GT Equivalence Verification (BPG18)
============================================================
GT: c0*P*sin(c1*t) + c2*(c3 - P/c4)*P + c5*P
Candidate formulas: 50

GT (fixed function):
\[
0.4770530111687279\,P\sin(0.7760602430275763\,t)\;+\;0.44545499474048156(1-\tfrac{P}{51.06128580599878})P\;+\;0.44545499474048156P
\]
Expand the polynomial part:
\[
0.44545499474048156(1-\tfrac{P}{51.06128580599878})P + 0.44545499474048156P
= (0.44545499474048156P - \tfrac{0.44545499474048156}{51.06128580599878}P^2) + 0.44545499474048156P
\]
So GT is exactly:
\[
\underbrace{-\alpha P^2}_{\text{quadratic in }P} \;+\;\underbrace{\beta P}_{\text{linear in }P}\;+\;\underbrace{\gamma P\sin(\omega t)}_{\text{P times sine in }t}
\]
with
- \(\gamma=0.4770530111687279\)
- \(\omega=0.7760602430275763\)
- \(\beta=0.8909099894809631\)
- \(\alpha=\frac{0.44545499474048156}{51.06128580599878}\neq 0\)

Thus any matching candidate must be able to represent **(i)** a \(P^2\) term with nonzero coefficient, **(ii)** a \(P\) term, and **(iii)** a \(P\sin(\omega t)\) term, and must avoid any extra dependence on \(t\) alone, \(\log|P|\), rational-in-\(P\) terms, exponentials, Max, etc., unless their coefficients can be set to 0.

---

### Candidate-by-candidate analysis

1. \(P^2c0 + P^2c1 + Pc2 + c3\sin(c4 t+c5)+ c6\log(\cdot)\sin(\cdot)\)  
   Can set \(c3=0, c6=0\) to remove extra terms, leaving only \(P^2\) and \(P\). But GT needs \(P\sin(\omega t)\). No \(P\sin\) term remains. **No match**.

2. \(P^2c0 + Pc1 + Pc2 + c3\exp(\cdot)+ c6\log(\cdot)\sin(\cdot)\)  
   Kill exp and log-sin by \(c3=0,c6=0\) → only \(P^2\) and \(P\), still missing \(P\sin(\omega t)\). **No match**.

3. \(P^2c0 e^{c1 t} + Pc2 + Pc3\sin(c4 t+c5)+ P c6/(c7+|P|)+ c8 t e^{c9 t}\)  
   To get a pure \(P^2\) term, need \(e^{c1 t}\) constant ⇒ \(c1=0\). Can set \(c6=0, c8=0\). Then we have \(P^2c0 + Pc2 + Pc3\sin(c4 t+c5)\), which matches GT form. Choose:
   - \(c0=-\alpha\)
   - \(c2=\beta\)
   - \(c3=\gamma\)
   - \(c4=\omega\)
   - \(c5=0\) (or any phase consistent; GT has no phase shift so set 0)
   **Match possible.**

4. \(Pc0\sin(c1+c2 t)+Pc3+Pc4/(P+c5)+Pc6/(P+c7)+c8 t^{c9}\)  
   Rational terms in \(P\) cannot become a polynomial \( -\alpha P^2\) for all \(P\) (unless coefficients 0). Setting \(c4=c6=0\) removes them, but then no \(P^2\) term exists. **No match**.

5. \(Pc0\sin(c1+c2 t)+Pc3+Pc4/(P+c5)+c6 t^{c7}+c8 e^{c9 t}\)  
   Remove non-GT terms by \(c4=c6=c8=0\) → only \(P\sin\) and \(P\), still no \(P^2\). **No match**.

6. \(Pc0 + c1 e^{c2/(c3+t)} + c4\max(0,P+c5)+ c6\log(\cdot)\sin(\cdot)\)  
   No way to produce \(P^2\) and \(P\sin(\omega t)\) simultaneously; max/log/exp are wrong. **No match**.

7. \(Pc0\sin(c1+c2 t)+P c3 e^{Pc4}+Pc5+Pc6/(P+c7)+c8 t^{c9}\)  
   Exponential in \(P\) and rational term must be zeroed: \(c3=0,c6=0,c8=0\). Then only \(P\sin\) and \(P\), no \(P^2\). **No match**.

8. \(P^2c0 e^{c1 t}+Pc2+Pc3\sin(\cdot)+c6 t e^{c7 t}+c8 e^{c9 t}\)  
   Need \(c1=0\) to make \(P^2\) term constant; set \(c6=0,c8=0\). Then identical reducible form as in (3): \(P^2c0+Pc2+Pc3\sin(\cdot)\). **Match possible** with same parameter choices.

9. \(Pc0\sin(c1+c2 t)+Pc3+P^{c4}c5\sin(\cdot)+c8 t^{c9}\)  
   To get \(P\sin\) term from \(P^{c4}c5\sin\), set \(c4=1\). But still no \(P^2\) term anywhere. **No match**.

10. \(Pc0 + c1 e^{c2/(c3+t)} + c4\log(\cdot)\sin(\cdot)+c8 e^{c9 t}\)  
   Lacks \(P^2\) and lacks \(P\sin\) (log term depends on \(P\) nonlinearly). **No match**.

11. \(Pc0\sin(\cdot)+Pc3+Pc4+Pc5 e^{Pc6}+c7 t^{c8}+c9\)  
   No \(P^2\). **No match**.

12. \(Pc0 + P^{c1}c2\sin(\cdot)+c5 t^2+c6 t+c7+c8/(c9|P|+1)\)  
   Can set \(c5=c6=c7=c8=0\). Then \(Pc0 + P^{c1}c2\sin(\cdot)\). Choose \(c1=1\) to make \(P\sin\). Still no \(P^2\). **No match**.

13. \(Pc0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3 t^2+c4 t+c5+c6\sin(c7\log(\cdot)+c9)\)  
   No \(P^2\) and extra \(t\)-only terms unless zeroed; even then no \(P^2\). **No match**.

14. \(Pc0 + Pc1\sin(c2 t+c3)+c4+c5 t^{c6}\)  
   No \(P^2\). **No match**.

15. \(Pc0 e^{c1|P|}+Pc2+c3\sin(\cdot)+c6\sin(\log(\cdot))\)  
   No \(P^2\); also \(c3\sin(\cdot)\) is not multiplied by \(P\). **No match**.

16. \(Pc0\sin(\cdot)+Pc3+c4 t^{c5}+c6 t^{c7}\cos(\cdot)\)  
   No \(P^2\). **No match**.

17. \(Pc0\sin(\cdot)+Pc3+Pc4 e^{Pc5}+c6\max(0,P+c7)+c8 t^{c9}\)  
   No \(P^2\) polynomial term; exp/max wrong. **No match**.

18. \(Pc0\sin(\cdot)+Pc3+c4 t^{c5}+c6 e^{Pc7}\sin(\cdot)\)  
   No \(P^2\). **No match**.

19. \(Pc0\sin(\cdot)+Pc3+c4 t^{c5}+c6 e^{c7\sin(\cdot)}\)  
   No \(P^2\). **No match**.

20. \(Pc0 + c1 e^{c2/(c3+t)} + c4\log(\cdot)\sin(\cdot)\)  
   No \(P^2\) and no clean \(P\sin\). **No match**.

21. \(P^2c0 e^{c1 t}+P^2c2\sin(\cdot)+Pc5+c6 e^{c7/(c8+t)}+c9\)  
   To avoid \(t\)-dependent coefficient on \(P^2\), need \(c1=0\). But then there is an unavoidable \(P^2\sin(\cdot)\) term unless \(c2=0\). Setting \(c2=0\) removes sine entirely (no \(P\sin\)). Also exp/constant must be zeroed. **No match**.

22. \(Pc0 e^{c1 t}+P^{c2}c3 e^{c4 t}+c5\sin(\cdot)\)  
   No \(P^2\) polynomial term; also sine not multiplied by \(P\). **No match**.

23. \(P^2c0 + Pc1\sin(c2+c3 t)+Pc4+Pc5/(P+c6)+Pc7+c8 t^{c9}\)  
   Set \(c5=0, c8=0\). Then \(P^2c0 + P[c1\sin(c2+c3 t)+c4+c7]\). This matches GT by choosing:
   - \(c0=-\alpha\)
   - \(c1=\gamma\)
   - \(c2=0\)
   - \(c3=\omega\)
   - \(c4+c7=\beta\) (split arbitrarily)
   **Match possible.**

24. \(P^2c0 + Pc1\sin(\cdot)+Pc4+Pc5\log(1+c6/P)+Pc7+c8 t^{c9}\)  
   Must set \(c5=0, c8=0\). Remaining can match as in (23). **Match possible.**

25. \(P^2c0 + P^2c1 + Pc2\sin(\cdot)+c5 t e^{c6 t}\)  
   Set \(c5=0\). Then \(P^2(\cdot)+P\sin(\cdot)\) but **no linear \(P\) term**. Cannot create \(\beta P\). **No match**.

   No \(P\sin\). **No match**.

   No \(P^2\), no \(P\sin\). **No match**.

   No \(P\) dependence at all. **No match**.

   Sine term is not multiplied by \(P\). If set \(c4=0\), lose sine entirely. **No match**.

   Sine not multiplied by \(P\). Also extra \(P^{c3}e^{P c5}\) must be killed by \(c4=0\). Then no \(P\sin\). **No match**.

   Sine not multiplied by \(P\). If \(c2=0\), lose sine. **No match**.

   No \(P^2\), no \(P\sin\). **No match**.

   No polynomial in \(P\) and wrong dependence. **No match**.

   Wrong \(P\) dependence. **No match**.

38. \(Pc0+c1 e^{c2/(c3+t)}+c4 e^{c5\sin(\cdot)}\)  
   No \(P^2\), no \(P\sin\). **No match**.

39. \(Pc0 e^{c1 t}+Pc2\log(c3/(P+c4)+1)+c5\sin(\cdot)\)  
   No \(P^2\); sine not multiplied by \(P\). **No match**.

40. \(P^2c0+P^2c1+Pc2+Pc3\sin(\cdot)+c6\sin(\cdot)\)  
   Set \(c6=0\). Then \(P^2(\cdot)+Pc2+P c3\sin(\cdot)\), exactly GT form. Choose:
   - \(c0+c1=-\alpha\) (split arbitrarily)
   - \(c2=\beta\)
   - \(c3=\gamma\)
   - \(c4=\omega\)
   - \(c5=0\)
   **Match possible.**

41. \(P^2c0+P^2c1+Pc2+c3\sin(\cdot)+c6 e^{c7\sin(\cdot)}\)  
   Sine term not multiplied by \(P\). If set \(c3=0\) and try to use the exp-of-sin term, it still isn’t \(P\sin\). **No match**.

42. \(P^2c0/(c1\cos(c2 t)+c3)+Pc4+c5 t/(c6+t^2)\)  
   To make \(P^2\) coefficient constant, need denominator constant: set \(c1=0\) so it becomes \(P^2(c0/c3)\). Also must remove \(t\)-only rational term: set \(c5=0\). Then expression is \(P^2(\text{const})+Pc4\), missing \(P\sin\). **No match**.

43. \(Pc0\sin(c1 t+c2)+Pc3+Pc4/(P+c5)+Pc6+c7\sin(\cdot)\)  
   No \(P^2\). **No match**.

   No \(P\sin\) and extra \(t\)-only terms. **No match**.

   \(P^2\) term is multiplied by \(\sin\), unlike GT. If set that sine to constant by forcing frequency 0, then the \(P\sin\) term also becomes \(P\cdot\text{const}\), losing required \(P\sin(\omega t)\). **No match**.

46. \(Pc0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3\sin(c4 t+c5)\)  
   No \(P^2\) and extra sine not times \(P\). **No match**.

   Must set \(c2=0\) to avoid \(P^2\sin\), and \(c6=0\) to avoid sine not times \(P\). Then no \(P\sin\). **No match**.

48. \(Pc0\sin(\cdot)+c3 t^2+c4 t+c5+c6 e^{c7 t}\log(\cdot)\)  
   No \(P^2\). **No match**.

   No \(P^2\). Also has \(t\)-dependent coefficients on \(P\) unless special limits; cannot become constant for all \(t\) while keeping other structure. **No match**.

GT: c0*P*sin(c1*t) + c2*(c3 - P/c4)*P + c5*P

Matched candidates: ["P**2*c0*exp(c1*t) + P*c2 + P*c3*sin(c4*t + c5) + P*c6/(c7 + Abs(P)) + c8*t*exp(c9*t)", "P**2*c0*exp(c1*t) + P*c2 + P*c3*sin(c4*t + c5) + c6*t*exp(c7*t) + c8*exp(c9*t)", "P**2*c0 + P*c1*sin(c2 + c3*t) + P*c4 + P*c5/(P + c6) + P*c7 + c8*t**c9", "P**2*c0 + P**2*c1 + P*c2 + P*c3*sin(c4*t + c5) + c6*sin(c7*t + c8)"]

I need to compare each candidate to the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT:** `0.4771*P*sin(0.7761*t) + 0.4455*(1 - P/51.06)*P + 0.4455*P`

Let me expand the GT:
`0.4771*P*sin(0.7761*t) + 0.4455*P - 0.4455*P²/51.06 + 0.4455*P`
`= 0.4771*P*sin(0.7761*t) + 0.8909*P - 0.008726*P²`

So GT = **c_a*P*sin(c_b*t) + c_c*P + c_d*P²** where c_d is negative.

The GT has three basis function types: P*sin(ωt), P, and P².

Let me check each candidate:

**Candidate 1:** `P²*c0 + P²*c1 + P*c2 + c3*sin(c4*t+c5) + c6*log(c7*|P|+1)*sin(c8*t+c9)`
Has `sin(t)` without P multiplier and `log(|P|+1)*sin(t)` instead of `P*sin(t)`. These are different basis functions. `log(c7*|P|+1)` ≠ `c*P` for all P. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 2:** Has `exp(c4/(c5+t))` and `log(c7*|P|+1)*sin(t)`. The exponential in t can't be zeroed without losing terms, and log≠P. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 3:** `P²*c0*exp(c1*t) + P*c2 + P*c3*sin(c4*t+c5) + P*c6/(c7+|P|) + c8*t*exp(c9*t)`
Set c1=0: P²*c0. Set c8=0: removes t*exp. Then: P²*c0 + P*c2 + P*c3*sin(c4*t+c5) + P*c6/(c7+|P|). The term P*c6/(c7+|P|) = P*c6/(c7+P) for P≥0. This is not a polynomial in P. Can we set c6=0? Then we get P²*c0 + P*c2 + P*c3*sin(c4*t+c5). This matches GT structure! With c5=0. **[MATCH]**

**Candidate 4:** `P*c0*sin(c1+c2*t) + P*c3 + P*c4/(P+c5) + P*c6/(P+c7) + c8*t^c9`
Set c8=0, and P*c4/(P+c5) + P*c6/(P+c7). Can these combine to give P²*constant? P*c4/(P+c5) = c4*P/(P+c5). With common denominator: [c4*P*(P+c7) + c6*P*(P+c5)] / [(P+c5)(P+c7)]. This is rational, not polynomial. Set c4=0, c6=0: then P*c0*sin + P*c3, missing P². **[NO MATCH]**

Wait, let me reconsider. P*c4/(P+c5): if c5→∞, this approaches 0. If c5=0: c4*P/P = c4, a constant. That doesn't help either. We need a P² term. Actually, P*c4/(P+c5) can be rewritten as c4*(P+c5-c5)/(P+c5)*P... no. Let me try: set c6=0, c8=0. Then P*c0*sin(c1+c2*t) + P*c3 + P*c4/(P+c5). P²/(P+c5) is not polynomial. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 5:** Similar to 4 with P*c4/(P+c5). Set c6=0, c8=0: P*sin + P + P²/(P+c5). Not polynomial. **[NO MATCH]**

Let me continue checking systematically for candidates that can produce exactly P², P, P*sin(ωt):

**Candidate 23:** `P²*c0 + P*c1*sin(c2+c3*t) + P*c4 + P*c5/(P+c6) + P*c7 + c8*t^c9`

**Candidate 34:** `P²*c0 + P*c1 + c2*sin(c3*t+c4)`. Missing P factor on sin term. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 40:** `P²*(c0+c1) + P*c2 + P*c3*sin(c4*t+c5) + c6*sin(c7*t+c8)`. Set c6=0: matches! **[MATCH]**

**Candidate 43:** P*c0*sin + P*(c3+c6) + P*c4/(P+c5) + c7*sin. Set c4=0, c7=0: P*sin + P. Missing P². **[NO MATCH]**
